class="navigationWrapper"><div class="navigationWrapper css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"></div></div></div></div><div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>Accept PayPal, credit, and debit card payments in a web or native experience using the PayPal Mobile Android SDK. Use customizable PayPal buttons with your custom checkout UI to align with your business branding. For more implementation details, see the </span><a href="https://github.com/paypal/paypal-android/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="_blank" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>PayPal GitHub repository</span></a><span>.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div><div id="know-before-you-code" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><h2 id="know-before-you-code" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#know-before-you-code" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#know-before-you-code" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Know before you code</h2><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>You need a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/accounts/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>developer account</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to get sandbox credentials:</span></p><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>PayPal uses REST API credentials which you can get from the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/dashboard/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>developer dashboard</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Client ID: Authenticates your account with PayPal and identifies an app in your sandbox.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Client secret: Authorizes an app in your sandbox. Keep this secret safe and dont share it.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Read</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Get started with PayPal APIs</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>for more information.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>You need a combination of PayPal and third-party tools:</span></p><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><a href="https://github.com/paypal/paypal-android" class="dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;position:relative;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Android SDK</span></a><span>: Adds PayPal-supported payment methods for Android.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Orders REST API</span></a><span>: Create, update, retrieve, authorize, and capture orders.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px36px;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Use Postman to explore and test PayPal APIs.</span></p><span>

id="before-you-begin-your-integration" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">1</span><h2 id="before-you-begin-your-integration" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#before-you-begin-your-integration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#before-you-begin-your-integration" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Before you begin your integration</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p></p><span>
</span><h3>Check your account setup for advanced card payments</h3><span>
</span><p><span>This integration requires a sandbox business account with the Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments capability. Your account should automatically have this capability.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>To confirm that Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments are enabled for you, check your sandbox business account as follows:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
</span><li><span>Log into the </span><a href="/dashboard/" class="undefined dx-external-href" target="" title="external link" rel="noopener noreferrer"><strong><span>PayPal Developer Dashboard</span></strong></a><span>, toggle </span><strong><span>Sandbox</span></strong><span>, and go to </span><strong><span>Apps & Credentials</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>In </span><strong><span>REST API apps</span></strong><span>, select the name of your app.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>Go to </span><strong><span>Features</span></strong><span> &gt; </span><strong><span>Accept payments</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span><li><span>Select the </span><strong><span>Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments</span></strong><span> checkbox and select </span><strong><span>Save Changes</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="contextual-alert"><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq steps</span></a><span>.</span></p></div></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p></p><span>
</span><h3>Check 3D Secure requirements</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Add 3D Secure to reduce the chance of fraud and improve the payment experience by authenticating a cardholder through their card issuer.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>Visit our </span><a href="/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/3d-secure/" target="_blank"><span>3D Secure</span></a><span> page to see if 3D Secure is required in your region and learn more about implementing 3DS in your app.</span></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><div class="dx-anchor newArchetype numberedWrapper"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">2</span><h2 id="integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="dx-anchor newArchetype"> <span id="#integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#integrate-the-sdk-into-your-app" class="dx-anchor__icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Integrate the SDK into your app</h2></div></div></div><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>The PayPal Mobile SDK is available through Maven Central. id="payment-integrations" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div style="margin-bottom:24px;margin-top:24px"><div class="numberedHeader-Section"><span class="NumberedHeader-module_archHeading__RUrq2">3</span><h2 id="payment-integrations" class="dx-anchor dx-content-subtitle newArchetype"> <span id="#payment-integrations" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#payment-integrations" class="dx-anchor__icon custom-anchor-icon numbered-icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Payment integrations</h2></div><div><div class="InstructionalStep-module_content__yK3Qw"><div class="ecmWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p></p><span>
</span><p><span>Integrate 3 different types of payments using the PayPal Mobile SDK:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
</span><li><strong><span>Card payments:</span></strong><span> Add card fields that align with your branding.</span></li><span>
</span><li><strong><span>PayPal native payments:</span></strong><span> Launch a checkout page within your app, instead of a popup.</span></li><span>
</span><li><strong><span>PayPal web payments:</span></strong><span> A lighter integration that launches a checkout page in a browser within your app.</span></li><span>
</span></ul></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><span>
</span><h3>Card</h3><span>
</span><h3 id="integrate-with-card-payments" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#integrate-with-card-payments" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#integrate-with-card-payments" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> Integrate with card payments</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Build and customize the card fields to align with your branding.</span></p><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="1-add-card-payments-module-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-add-card-payments-module-to-your-app" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-add-card-payments-module-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> 1. Add card payments module to your app</h3><span>
</span><p><span>Add the </span><code class=""><span>card-payments</span></code><span> package dependency in your app's </span><code class=""><span>build.gradle</span></code><span> file:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">dependencies </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">{</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">  implementation </span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">3</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token </span><h3 id="2-create-cardclient" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-create-cardclient" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-create-cardclient" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> </h3><p><br/></p><h3 id="2-create-cardclient" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-create-cardclient" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-create-cardclient" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Create CardClient</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A </span><code class=""><span>CardClient</span></code><span> helps you attach a card to a payment.</span></p><span>
</span><p><span>In your Android app:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Use the </span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_ID</span></code><span> to construct a </span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Construct a </span><code class=""><span>CardClient</span></code><span> using your </span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span> object.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">val config </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">CoreConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;CLIENT_ID&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"> environment </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> Environment</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">.</span><span class="token plain">SANDBOX</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain" style="display:inline-block">
</span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">3</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">val cardClient </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">CardClient</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token plain">config</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
</span><h3 id="3-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-get-order-id" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> </h3><p><br/></p><h3 id="3-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-get-order-id" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->3. Get Order ID</h3><span>
</span><p><span>On your server:</span></p><span>
</span><ol><span>
    </span><li><span>Create an </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span> by using the </span><a href="/docs/api/orders/v2" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Pass your </span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span> in the </span><code class=""><span>Authorization</span></code><span> header. To get an </span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span>, use the </span><a href="https:/api/rest/authentication/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Authentication API</span></a><span>.</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
            </span><p><strong><span>Note:</span></strong><span> This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to </span><a href="https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token" class="dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1"><span>https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
        </span></span></div></div><span>
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Pass the </span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span>. You'll need to pass either </span><code class=""><span>AUTHORIZE</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>CAPTURE</span></code><span> as the </span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span> type. This type must match the </span><code class=""><span>/authorize</span></code><span> or </span><code class=""><span>/capture</span></code><span> endpoint you use to process your order.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p><span>When a buyer starts a payment, send the </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span> from your server to your client app.</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="4-create-card-request" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#4-create-card-request" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#4-create-card-request" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> 4. Create card request</h3><span>
</span><p><span>A </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> object:</span></p><span>
</span><ul><span>
    </span><li><span>Attaches a card to an </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li><span>Launches 3D Secure when a payment requires additional authentication.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="1-collect-card-payment-details" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-collect-card-payment-details" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-collect-card-payment-details" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. Collect card payment details</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Build a </span><code class=""><span>card</span></code><span> object with the buyer's card details:</span></p><span>

</span><p><span>Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.</span></p><span>
</span><h4 id="2-build-cardrequest" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-build-cardrequest" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-build-cardrequest" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- --> </h4><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="2-build-cardrequest" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-build-cardrequest" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-build-cardrequest" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Build CardRequest</h4><span>
</span><p><span>Build a </span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span> with the </span><code class=""><span>card</span></code><span> object and your </span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" default value is SCA.SCA_WHEN_REQUIRED</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">6</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem"><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/nvp-soap/payflow/3d-secure-overview/" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>3D Secure</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is supported for all card payments to comply with the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/uk/webapps/mpp/PSD2?_ga=1.18434873.1625369690.1652045188" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Second Payment Services Directive (PSD2)</span></a><span>. PSD2 is a European Union regulation that introduces</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://www.ukfinance.org.uk/our-expertise/payments-and-innovation/strong-customer-authentication" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Strong Customer Authentication (SCA)</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>and other security requirements.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem"><span>Select your SCA launch option type using the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>sca</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>parameter in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>initializer:</span></p><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><code class=""><span>SCA.SCA_WHEN_REQUIRED</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>launches an SCA challenge when applicable. This is enabled by default.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><code class=""><span>SCA.SCA_ALWAYS</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>requires an SCA challenge for all card transactions.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><h4 id="3-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->3. Set up your app for browser switching</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem"><span>The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>sca</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>challenge launches in a browser within your application. Your app needs to handle the browser switch between the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>sca</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>challenge and the checkout page. Set up a return URL that returns to your app from the browser.</span></p><span>
</span><h4 id="4-create-a-return-url" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#4-create-a-return-url" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#4-create-a-return-url" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->4. Create a return URL</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem"><span>Provide a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>returnUrl</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>so the browser returns to your application after the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>sca</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>challenge finishes.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem"><span>The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>returnUrl</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>should have the following format:</span></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><p><br/><span>


</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">myapp</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">:</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">/</span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">/</span><span class="token plain">return_url</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>myapp://</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>portion of the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>returnUrl</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is a custom URL scheme that you need to register in your app's</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>AndroidManifest.xml</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="5-add-card-payment-activity-to-the-android-manifest" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#5-add-card-payment-activity-to-the-android-manifest" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#5-add-card-payment-activity-to-the-android-manifest" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->5. Add card payment activity to the Android manifest</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Update your app's</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>AndroidManifest.xml</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>with details about the card payment activity that will return the user to your app after completing the SCA check. Include the following elements:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Set the activity</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>launchMode</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>singleTop</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Set the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>android:scheme</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>on the Activity that will be responsible for handling the deep link back into the app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Add an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent-filter</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Register the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>myapp://</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>custom URL scheme in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent-filter</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><span>Note:</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>android:exported</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is required if your app compile SDK version is API 31 (Android 12) or later.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>

</span><h4 id="6-connect-the-card-payment-activity" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#6-connect-the-card-payment-activity" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#6-connect-the-card-payment-activity" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->6. Connect the card payment activity</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Add</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onNewIntent</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to your activity:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div </span><p><br/><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="5-approve-order" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#5-approve-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#5-approve-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->5. Approve order</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>After your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CardRequest</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>has the card details, call</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>cardClient.approveOrder()</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to process the payment.</span></p><span>

</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="7-authorize-and-capture-order" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#7-authorize-and-capture-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#7-authorize-and-capture-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <br class="Apple-interchange-newline"/>7. Authorize and capture order</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Submit your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onApproveOrderSuccess</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>method.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Call the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><code class=""><span>authorize</span></code></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="sample-request-authorize-order" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sample-request-authorize-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sample-request-authorize-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Sample request: Authorize order</h4><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn </span><h3 id="8-test-integration" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#8-test-integration" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#8-test-integration" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->8. Test integration</h3><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Before going live, test your integration in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>sandbox environment</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Learn more about the following resources on the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Card Testing</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>page:</span></p><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Use</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>test card numbers</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to simulate successful payments for Expanded Checkout integrations.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Use</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-rejectiontriggers" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>rejection triggers</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to simulate card error scenarios.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Test</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-simulate3dsecurecardpayments" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>3D Secure authentication</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>scenarios.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Test your integration by following</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testintegration" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>these recommended use cases</span></a><span>. See the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>for details about billing address fields and other parameters. For example, use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/reference/country-codes/" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>2-character country code</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to test the billing address.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>Use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-creditcardgenerator" class="undefined dx-external-href" pa-marked="1" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>credit card generator</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to generate additional test credit cards for sandbox testing.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>When prompted for required data for the sandbox business request, such as a phone number, enter any number that fits the required format. Because this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Before you go live, you'll need to complete</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/entry/product/ppcp" class="dx-external-href dx-external-href" rel="noopener noreferrer" title="external link" target="_blank" pa-marked="1" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;position:relative"><span>live onboarding</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to be eligible to process cards with your live PayPal account.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="" class="multipartyTabs"><div class="css-165s6em-layout_container" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-s8u2ug-row" data-ppui-info="grid_3.3.6__7.46.3"><div class="css-1nhh7rf-col" data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h2 id="native-payments" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#native-payments" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#native-payments" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Native Payments</h2><span>
</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>


    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Deprecation notice:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>The</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePayments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>module is deprecated since July 2024. Updates and bug fixes end in July 2025. We recommend to use the </span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebPayments</span></code><span> module instead. To migrate from </span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePayments</span></code><span> to </span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebPayments</span></code><span>, follow the steps in </span><a href="#web-payments" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="" rel="noopener noreferrer"><span>Web payments</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>

</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><h3 id="use-paypal-native-payments" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#use-paypal-native-payments" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#use-paypal-native-payments" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Use PayPal native payments</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Use</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePayments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to add a PayPal paysheet to your app. The paysheet is a checkout page that the client launches within your app, instead of showing up as a pop-up. The paysheet shows all the PayPal payment methods available and helps the payer complete their payment.</span></p><span>
</span><h4 id="native-checkout-for-a-first-time-customer" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#native-checkout-for-a-first-time-customer" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#native-checkout-for-a-first-time-customer" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Native checkout for a first-time customer</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_01.png" alt="img" style="box-sizing:inherit;border:0pxnone;vertical-align:middle;max-width:100%"/><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_02.png" alt="img" style="box-sizing:inherit;border:0pxnone;vertical-align:middle;max-width:100%"/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="native-checkout-for-a-returning-customer" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#native-checkout-for-a-returning-customer" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#native-checkout-for-a-returning-customer" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Native checkout for a returning customer</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><img src="https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-repeat-time-flow.png" alt="img" style="box-sizing:inherit;border:0pxnone;vertical-align:middle;max-width:100%;display:block;margin:0pxauto"/></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Follow these steps to add</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePayments</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="1-add-paypalnativepayments-module-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-add-paypalnativepayments-module-to-your-app" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-add-paypalnativepayments-module-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Add the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>paypal-native-payments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>package dependency in your app's</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>build.gradle</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>file:</span></p><span>
