</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="2-enable-native-checkout-sdk" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-enable-native-checkout-sdk" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-enable-native-checkout-sdk" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Enable Native Checkout SDK</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>You'll need to set up authorization to use the Native Checkout SDK. To create a client ID and secret, follow the steps in</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/#link-getstarted" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Get Started</span></a><span>. You need these values to generate an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><h4 id="sandbox-business-account" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sandbox-business-account" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sandbox-business-account" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Sandbox business account</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Set up your sandbox business account to use native checkout as follows:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Log into the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/dashboard/" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>PayPal Developer Dashboard</span></strong></a><span>, toggle</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Sandbox</span></strong><span>, and go to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Apps & Credentials</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>In</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>REST API apps</span></strong><span>, select the name of your app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Go to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Features</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>&gt;</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Accept payments</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>and select</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>*Native Checkout SDK</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Select</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Save Changes</span></strong><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><h4 id="add-return-url" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#add-return-url" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#add-return-url" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Add return URL</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>A return URL redirects users to the app after authenticating. Use the following steps to create a return URL:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Select your app from the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>My Apps & Credentials</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>page on the Developer Dashboard.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Go to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Features</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>&gt;</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Other features</span></strong><span>. Select the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Log in with PayPal</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>checkbox. Click on</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Advanced Settings</span></strong><span>. A pop-up window will open, and you'll see the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Return URL</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>field in the new window.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>You can use an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.android.com/training/app-links" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Android App Link</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>registered within the Developer Console to handle SDK redirects.</span></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Alternatively, you can use your application ID (typically referenced via</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>BuildConfig.APPLICATION_ID</span></code><span>) and register your return URL with</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>://paypalpay</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>as the suffix. For example, if your application ID is</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>com.paypal.app</span></code><span>, input</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>com.paypal.app://paypalpay</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>as the return URL.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>The return URL in the Developer Dashboard and the SDK must match exactly.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>The application ID and return URL must use lower case letters. The return URL is passed to the SDK via an intent filter and</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/data-element#:~:text=Host%20name%20matching%20in%20the%20Android%20framework%20is%20case%2Dsensitive%2C%20unlike%20the%20formal%20RFC.%20As%20a%20result%2C%20always%20specify%20host%20names%20using%20lowercase%20letters" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>host name matching in the Android framework is case-sensitive</span></a></li><span>
</span></ul><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>If you change the return URL in the Developer Dashboard, PayPal must review your app again. The review period automatically begins any time the return URL changes.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><ol start="3" style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Select the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif;margin-top:0px;padding-top:0px"><span>Full Name</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>and</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Email</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>checkboxes found within the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Advanced Settings</span></strong><span>. These are scopes of the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/identity/v1/" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Identity API</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="3-create-paypalnativecheckoutclient" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-create-paypalnativecheckoutclient" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-create-paypalnativecheckoutclient" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->3. Create PayPalNativeCheckoutClient</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Use the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="1-construct-coreconfig" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-construct-coreconfig" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-construct-coreconfig" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. Construct CoreConfig</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>In your Android app, use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to construct a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div </span><h4 id="3-set-up-payment-listener" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-set-up-payment-listener" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-set-up-payment-listener" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->3. Set up payment listener</h4><span>

</span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="4-listen-for-shipping-details" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#4-listen-for-shipping-details" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#4-listen-for-shipping-details" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->4. Listen for shipping details</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>When a payer chooses to use shipping details from their PayPal profile, use</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativeShippingListener</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to listen for changes to their shipping address or shipping method.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>You can only implement</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativeShippingListener</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>if the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#definition-experience_context_base" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><code class=""><span>shipping_preference</span></code></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>in the order ID is set to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>GET_FROM_FILE.</span></code></p><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>Skip this step if you created your order ID with the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>shipping_preference</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>set to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>NO_SHIPPING</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Set a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>shippingListener</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>on the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativeCheckoutClient</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to send notifications to your app when the user updates their shipping address or shipping method.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>This code sample uses a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>trycatch</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>function to handle the response:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><p></p><span>

</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="5-modify-shipping-details" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#5-modify-shipping-details" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#5-modify-shipping-details" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->5. Modify shipping details</h4><span>
</span><p></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>When the shipping method changes, update the order details on your server by sending a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PATCH</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>request to the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><span>Update order</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders API.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Approve or reject changes to the shipping information to see changes appear in the paysheet UI by calling either</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePaysheetActions.approve()</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativePaysheetActions.reject()</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>To update the paysheet with a new shipping method, or when</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onPayPalNativeShippingMethodChange</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is called:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Patch the order on your server using the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>replace</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>operation with all shipping methods.</span><ul style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:0px;margin-bottom:1.5rem"><span>
            </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Mark the new shipping method as selected.</span></li><span>
            </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Optional: Update the amount to reflect the new shipping cost.</span></li><span>
        </span></ul><span>
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Call</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>approve()</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>reject()</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to accept or reject the changes and continue the payment flow.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>For more information, visit the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>Update order</span></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders v2 API.</span></p><span>
</span><h3 id="4-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#4-get-order-id" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#4-get-order-id" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->4. Get Order ID</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>On your server:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Create an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>by using the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Pass your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>Authorization</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>header. To get an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span>, use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/authentication/" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><span>Authentication API</span></a><span>.</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
            </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
        </span></span></div></div><span>
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Pass the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span>. You'll need to pass either</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>AUTHORIZE</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CAPTURE</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>as the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>type. This type must match the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>/authorize</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>/capture</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint you use to process your order.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><p><br/></p></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>When a buyer starts a payment, send the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>from your server to your client app.</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><h3 id="5-start-paypal-native-payments-flow" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#5-start-paypal-native-payments-flow" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#5-start-paypal-native-payments-flow" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->5. Start PayPal Native Payments flow</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>To start the PayPal Native Payments flow, call the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>startCheckout</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>function in</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativeCheckoutClient</span></code><span>, with a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalNativeCheckoutRequest</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" </span><p><span>
</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><h3 id="6-authorize-and-capture-order" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#6-authorize-and-capture-order" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#6-authorize-and-capture-order" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->6. Authorize and capture order</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Submit your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onPayPalSuccess</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>method.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Call the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><code class=""><span>authorize</span></code></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><h4 id="sample-request-authorize-order-1" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sample-request-authorize-order-1" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sample-request-authorize-order-1" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Sample request: Authorize order</h4><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>

</span></p><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Call the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><code class=""><span>capture</span></code></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><h4 id="sample-request-capture-order-1" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sample-request-capture-order-1" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sample-request-capture-order-1" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Sample request: Capture order</h4><p><br/></p><p></p><span>

data-ppui="true"><div class="codeTabsWrapper"><div class="ecmRichText" style="margin-bottom:0px"><h2 id="web-payments" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#web-payments" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#web-payments" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Web payments</h2><span>
</span><h3 id="paypal-web-payments" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#paypal-web-payments" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#paypal-web-payments" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->PayPal Web Payments</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Integrate</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebPayments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to add a lighter checkout integration to your app. The checkout experience is launched in a browser within your application, reducing the size of the SDK.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Follow these steps to integrate</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebPayments</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="1-add-paypalwebpayments-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-add-paypalwebpayments-to-your-app" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-add-paypalwebpayments-to-your-app" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. Add PayPalWebPayments to your app</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Add the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>paypal-web-payments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>package dependency in your app's</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>build.gradle</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>file:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">2</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">      implementation </span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;com.paypal.android:paypal-web-payments:CURRENT-VERSION&quot;</span><span class="token plain"></span></span></div><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">3</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">    </span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">}</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="2-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-set-up-your-app-for-browser-switching" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Set up your app for browser switching</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><code class=""><span>PayPalWebPayments</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>launches a checkout page in a browser within your application. Your app needs to handle the browser switch between the checkout page and your app. Set up a return URL that returns to your app from the browser.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Update your app's</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>AndroidManifest.xml</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>with details about the card payment activity that will return the user to your app after completing the payment. Include the following elements:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Set the activity</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>launchMode</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>singleTop</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Set the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>android:scheme</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>on the Activity that will be responsible for handling the deep link back into the app.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Add an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent-filter</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Register the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>myapp://</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>custom URL scheme in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent-filter</span></code><span>.</span></li><span>
</span></ol><span>
</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><span>Note:</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>android:exported</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>is required if your app compile SDK version is API 31 (Android 12) or later.</span></p><span>
</span></span></div></div><span>

</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Also, add</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onNewIntent</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to the host activity in your app:</span></p><span>

</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="3-create-paypalwebcheckoutclient" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#3-create-paypalwebcheckoutclient" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#3-create-paypalwebcheckoutclient" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->3. Create PayPalWebCheckoutClient</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Use the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:</span></p><span>
</span><h4 id="1-construct-coreconfig-1" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#1-construct-coreconfig-1" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#1-construct-coreconfig-1" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->1. Construct CoreConfig</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>In your Android app, use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CLIENT_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to construct a</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CoreConfig</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">val config </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token function" style="color:rgb(220, 220, 170)">CoreConfig</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">(</span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;CLIENT_ID&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">,</span><span class="token plain"> environment </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> Environment</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">.</span><span class="token plain">SANDBOX</span><span class="token punctuation" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">)</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>
</span><p><br style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"/></p><span>
</span><h4 id="2-create-return-url" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#2-create-return-url" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#2-create-return-url" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->2. Create return URL</h4><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Set a return URL using the custom scheme you configured in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ActivityManifest.xml</span></code><span>:</span></p><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div style="gap:2em;display:flex;justify-content:space-between"><div class="CodeTabs-module_imageContainerBtn__42--0 CodeTabs-module_pad__kZS21" data-testid="copyButton"><div class="imageContainerBtn codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28 31.5523 27.5523 32 27 32L17 32C16.4477 32 16 31.5523 16 31V21C16 20.4477 16.4477 20 17 20L20 20L20 17C20 16.4477 20.4477 16 21 16H31C31.5523 16 32 16.4477 32 17L32 27C32 27.5523 31.5523 28 31 28H28ZM30.5 17.5L30.5 26.5H28L28 21C28 20.4477 27.5523 20 27 20L21.5 20L21.5 17.5L30.5 17.5Z" fill="#003087"></path></svg></div></div></div></div><div data-testid="content"><div data-testid="wrapper" class="CodeBlock-module_wrapper__-pzLU"><pre class="CodeBlock-module_codeBlock__yQGXn" data-testid="codeBlock" style="color:#9CDCFE;background-color:#1E1E1E"><div class="CodeBlock-module_line__Y6IZx" style="color:#9CDCFE" data-testid="line"><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineNumber__7WEdl" data-testid="lineNumber">1</span><span class="CodeBlock-module_lineContent__-DnJH" data-testid="lineContent"><span class="token plain">val returnUrl </span><span class="token operator" style="color:rgb(212, 212, 212)">=</span><span class="token plain"> </span><span class="token string" style="color:rgb(206, 145, 120)">&quot;custom-url-scheme&quot;</span></span></div></pre></div></div></div><span>

    </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.</span></p><span>

</span><p><br/></p><span>
</span><h3 id="4-get-order-id-1" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#4-get-order-id-1" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#4-get-order-id-1" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->4. Get Order ID</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>On your server:</span></p><span>
</span><ol style="box-sizing:inherit;margin-top:-1rem;margin-bottom:1.5rem;list-style-type:decimal;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Create an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>by using the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><span>Orders v2 API</span></a><span>.</span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Pass your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>in the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>Authorization</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>header. To get an</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ACCESS_TOKEN</span></code><span>, use the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/authentication/" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent;display:inline-block;white-space:normal;word-break:normal"><span>Authentication API</span></a><span>.</span><div role="alert" class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__1QhIq ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert--note__gRM6J"><div class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__header__T2Wkg"><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__icon__puACD css-4757ty-svg-size_xs" data-ppui-info="icons_8.21.2" role="img" aria-label="note" data-ppui="true"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="currentColor" viewBox="0 0 24 24" width="1em" height="1em" data-ppui="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M21 12a9 9 0 1 1-18 0 9 9 0 0 1 18 0zm-9.662 5h1.32c.18 0 .276-.096.276-.276v-5.925c0-.18-.096-.276-.276-.276h-1.32c-.18 0-.276.096-.276.276v5.925c0 .18.096.276.276.276zM12 9a1 1 0 1 0 0-2 1 1 0 0 0 0 2z" clip-rule="evenodd" data-ppui="true"></path></svg></span><span class="ContextualAlert-module_pp-alert__content__2-Ddi"><span>
            </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px"><strong style="box-sizing:inherit;font-weight:bolder;font-family:PayPalOpen-Bold,PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;PayPalSansBig&quot;,sans-serif"><span>Note:</span></strong><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><span>https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token</span></a><span>.</span></p><span>
        </span></span></div></div><span>
    </span></li><span>
    </span><li style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0.375rem0px"><span>Pass the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span>. You'll need to pass either</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>AUTHORIZE</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>CAPTURE</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>as the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>intent</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>type. This type must match the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>/authorize</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>or</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>/capture</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint you use to process your order.</span></li><span>
</span></ol></div><div class="codeBlockComponent"><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol </span><p><br/></p><h3 id="5-create-web-checkout-request" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#5-create-web-checkout-request" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#5-create-web-checkout-request" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->5. Create web checkout request</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Configure your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebCheckoutRequest</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>with the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span>. </span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Call</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>payPalWebCheckoutClient.start()</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>to process the payment.</span></p><span>

</span><p><br/></p><h3 id="7-authorize-and-capture-order-1" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#7-authorize-and-capture-order-1" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#7-authorize-and-capture-order-1" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->7. Authorize and capture order</h3><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Submit your</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>ORDER_ID</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>onPayPalWebSuccess</span></code><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>method on</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><code class=""><span>PayPalWebCheckoutListener</span></code><span>.</span></p><span>
</span><p style="box-sizing:inherit;margin:0px0px1.5rem;color:rgb(30,32,33);font-family:PayPalOpen-Regular,&quot;HelveticaNeue&quot;,Helvetica,Arial,sans-serif;font-size:16px;font-style:normal;font-variant-ligatures:normal;font-variant-caps:normal;font-weight:400;letter-spacing:normal;orphans:2;text-align:start;text-indent:0px;text-transform:none;widows:2;word-spacing:0px;-webkit-text-stroke-width:0px;white-space:normal;background-color:rgb(255,255,255);text-decoration-thickness:initial;text-decoration-style:initial;text-decoration-color:initial"><span>Call the</span><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><a href="https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize" class="undefined dx-external-href" title="external link" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" style="box-sizing:inherit;color:rgb(51,122,183);text-decoration:none;background-color:transparent"><code class=""><span>authorize</span></code></a><span><span>&nbsp;</span></span><span>endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:</span></p><span>
</span><p><br/></p><h4 id="sample-request-authorize-order-2" class="dx-anchor"> <span id="#sample-request-authorize-order-2" class="headingAnchorLinks"></span> <a href="#sample-request-authorize-order-2" class="dx-anchor__icon" aria-hidden="true" pa-marked="1" tabindex="-1"></a> <!-- -->Sample request: Authorize order</h4><span>
</span><div class="CodeTabs-module_tab__oLSKS" data-testid="tab"><div class="CodeTabs-module_nav__8zNfs" data-testid="nav"><ol class="CodeTabs-module_tabList__V3BAB" data-testid="tabList"></ol><div codeBlockButton"><svg width="48" height="48" viewBox="0 0 48 48" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style="cursor:pointer"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M28 28V31C28
