Payments in Android Apps with PayPal SDK","description":"Accept PayPal, credit, \u0026 debit card payments in Android apps using the PayPal SDK. Customize the checkout UI to align with your brand \u0026 improve user experience."},"language":["en-US"],"ecm":{"link":"https://internal.paypalinc.com/contentmanager/space/b7241346-cd3d-4e70-a1c7-74bfd4aaab3d/environment/ddea4eb4-f0c4-4321-aa67-654e40fe9a18/entries/1moPelqVZS84XH3wEM8fCf","envAllowsPreview":true},"markdownContent":"---\ntitle: Integrate card payments in Android\nslug: /docs/checkout/advanced/android/\ncreateTime: '2024-07-10T06:38:35.872Z'\nupdateTime: '2025-07-31T07:18:29.306Z'\n---\n\n\n# Integrate card payments in Android\n\nAccept PayPal, credit, and debit card payments in a web or native experience using the PayPal Mobile Android SDK. Use customizable PayPal buttons with your custom checkout UI to align with your business branding. For more implementation details, see the [PayPal GitHub repository](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-android/) .\n\n\n\n## Know before you code \nYou need a  [developer account](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/accounts/)  to get sandbox credentials:\n\n- PayPal uses REST API credentials which you can get from the  [developer dashboard](https://developer.paypal.com/dashboard/) .\n- Client ID: Authenticates your account with PayPal and identifies an app in your sandbox.\n- Client secret: Authorizes an app in your sandbox. Keep this secret safe and dont share it.\n\nRead  [Get started with PayPal APIs](https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/)  for more information.\n\nYou need a combination of PayPal and third-party tools:\n\n- [Android SDK](https://github.com/paypal/paypal-android) : Adds PayPal-supported payment methods for Android.\n- [Orders REST API](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/) : Create, update, retrieve, authorize, and capture orders.\n\nUse Postman to explore and test PayPal APIs.\n\n\n\n## Before you begin your integration \n\n\n### Check your account setup for advanced card payments\nThis integration requires a sandbox business account with the Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments capability. Your account should automatically have this capability.\n\nTo confirm that Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments are enabled for you, check your sandbox business account as follows:\n\n- Log into the [**PayPal Developer Dashboard**](/dashboard/) , toggle **Sandbox** , and go to **Apps \u0026 Credentials** .\n- In **REST API apps** , select the name of your app.\n- Go to **Features** \u0026gt; **Accept payments** .\n- Select the **Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments** checkbox and select **Save Changes** .\n\n\n**info**\n**Note:** If you created a sandbox business account through [sandbox.paypal.com](https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/?_ga=1.158343865.248280996.1670866755) , and the advanced credit and debit card payments status for the account is disabled, [complete the sandbox onboarding steps](https://www.sandbox.paypal.com/bizsignup/#/checkAccount) .\n\n\n\n\n### Check 3D Secure requirements\nAdd 3D Secure to reduce the chance of fraud and improve the payment experience by authenticating a cardholder through their card issuer.\n\nVisit our [3D Secure](/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/3d-secure/) page to see if 3D Secure is required in your region and learn more about implementing 3DS in your app.\n\n\nThe PayPal Mobile SDK is available through Maven Central. Add the mavenCentral repository to the build.gradle file of your project root:\n\n\n#### **`Integrate the SDK into your app Demo`**\n```javascript\nallprojects {\n  repositories {\n    mavenCentral()\n  }\n}    \n```\n### Snapshot builds\nYou can also use snapshot builds to test upcoming features before release. To include a snapshot build:\n\n\n#### 1. Add snapshots repository\nAdd the snapshots repository to the build.gradle file of your project root.\n\n\n#### **`Add snapshots repository`**\n```javascript\nallprojects {\n  repositories {\n    mavenCentral()\n    maven {\n      url 'https://oss.sonatype.org/content/repositories/snapshots/'\n    }\n  }\n}  \n```\n\n#### 2. Add snapshot to dependencies\nThen, add a snapshot build by adding -SNAPSHOT to the current dependency version. For example, if you want to add a snapshot build for CardPayments , add the following:\n\n\n#### **`Add snapshot to dependencies`**\n```javascript\ndependencies {\n  implementation 'com.paypal.android:card-payments:CURRENT-VERSION-SNAPSHOT'\n}\n```\n\n\n## Payment integrations \n\n\nIntegrate 3 different types of payments using the PayPal Mobile SDK:\n\n- **Card payments:** Add card fields that align with your branding.\n- **PayPal native payments:** Launch a checkout page within your app, instead of a popup.\n- **PayPal web payments:** A lighter integration that launches a checkout page in a browser within your app.\n\n\n### Card\n### Integrate with card payments\nBuild and customize the card fields to align with your branding.\n\n \n\n### 1. Add card payments module to your app\nAdd the card-payments package dependency in your app's build.gradle file:\n\ndependencies {\n  implementation \"com.paypal.android:card-payments:CURRENT-VERSION\"\n}### \n \n\n### 2. Create CardClient\nA CardClient helps you attach a card to a payment.\n\nIn your Android app:\n\n- Use the CLIENT_ID to construct a CoreConfig .\n- Construct a CardClient using your CoreConfig object.\n\nval config = CoreConfig(\"CLIENT_ID\", environment = Environment.SANDBOX)\n\nval cardClient = CardClient(config)### \n \n\n### 3. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an ORDER_ID by using the [Orders v2 API](/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your ACCESS_TOKEN in the Authorization header. To get an ACCESS_TOKEN , use the [Authentication API](https:/api/rest/authentication/) . **Note:** This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n \n- Pass the intent . You'll need to pass either AUTHORIZE or CAPTURE as the intent type. This type must match the /authorize or /capture endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n\n#### **`Sample request`**\n```javascript\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw '{\n    \"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",\n    \"purchase_units\": [\n      {\n        \"amount\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"5.00\"\n        }\n      }\n    ]\n  }'\n\n```\n\n\n#### **`Sample response`**\n```javascript\n\n{\n  \"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",\n  \"status\":\"CREATED\"\n}\n\n```\nWhen a buyer starts a payment, send the ORDER_ID from your server to your client app.\n\n### 4. Create card request\nA CardRequest object:\n\n- Attaches a card to an ORDER_ID .\n- Launches 3D Secure when a payment requires additional authentication.\n\n \n\n#### 1. Collect card payment details\nBuild a card object with the buyer's card details:\n\nval card = Card(\n  number = \"4005519200000004\",\n  expirationMonth = \"01\",\n  expirationYear = \"2025\",\n  securityCode = \"123\",\n  billingAddress = Address(\n    streetAddress = \"123 Main St.\",\n    extendedAddress = \"Apt. 1A\",\n    locality = \"Anytown\",\n    region = \"CA\",\n    postalCode = \"12345\",\n    countryCode = \"US\"\n  )\n)Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.\n\n#### \n \n\n#### 2. Build CardRequest\nBuild a CardRequest with the card object and your ORDER_ID :\n\nval cardRequest  = CardRequest(\n  orderID = \"ORDER_ID\",\n  card = card,\n  returnUrl = \"myapp://return_url\", // custom URL scheme needs to be configured in AndroidManifest.xml\n  sca = SCA.SCA_ALWAYS // default value is SCA.SCA_WHEN_REQUIRED\n)\n\n[3D Secure](https://developer.paypal.com/api/nvp-soap/payflow/3d-secure-overview/)  is supported for all card payments to comply with the  [Second Payment Services Directive (PSD2)](https://www.paypal.com/uk/webapps/mpp/PSD2?_ga=1.18434873.1625369690.1652045188) . PSD2 is a European Union regulation that introduces  [Strong Customer Authentication (SCA)](https://www.ukfinance.org.uk/our-expertise/payments-and-innovation/strong-customer-authentication)  and other security requirements.\n\nSelect your SCA launch option type using the  sca  parameter in the  CardRequest  initializer:\n\n- SCA.SCA_WHEN_REQUIRED  launches an SCA challenge when applicable. This is enabled by default.\n- SCA.SCA_ALWAYS  requires an SCA challenge for all card transactions.\n\n#### 3. Set up your app for browser switching\nThe  sca  challenge launches in a browser within your application. Your app needs to handle the browser switch between the  sca  challenge and the checkout page. Set up a return URL that returns to your app from the browser.\n\n#### 4. Create a return URL\nProvide a  returnUrl  so the browser returns to your application after the  sca  challenge finishes.\n\nThe  returnUrl  should have the following format:\n\n\n\n  \n\nmyapp://return_url\n\nThe  myapp://  portion of the  returnUrl  is a custom URL scheme that you need to register in your app's  AndroidManifest.xml .\n\n \n\n#### 5. Add card payment activity to the Android manifest\nUpdate your app's  AndroidManifest.xml  with details about the card payment activity that will return the user to your app after completing the SCA check. Include the following elements:\n\n- Set the activity  launchMode  to  singleTop .\n- Set the  android:scheme  on the Activity that will be responsible for handling the deep link back into the app.\n- Add an  intent-filter .\n- Register the  myapp://  custom URL scheme in the  intent-filter .\n\nNote:  android:exported  is required if your app compile SDK version is API 31 (Android 12) or later.\n\n \n\n\n\n\u0026lt;activity\n  android:name=\".MyCardPaymentActivity\"\n  android:launchMode=\"singleTop\"\n  android:exported=\"true\"\u0026gt;\n  \n  \u0026lt;intent-filter\u0026g;\n  \n    \u0026l;action android:name=\"android.intent.action.VIEW\" /\u0026gt;\n  \n    \u0026lt;data android:scheme=\"myapp\" /\u0026gt;\n  \n    \u0026lt;category android:name=\"android.intent.category.DEFAULT\" /\u0026gt;;\n  \n    \u0026lt;category android:name=\"android.intent.category.BROWSABLE\" /\u0026gt;\n  \n  \u0026lt;/intent-filter\u0026gt;\n  \n\u0026lt;/activity\u0026gt;\n\n \n\n#### 6. Connect the card payment activity\nAdd  onNewIntent  to your activity:\n\n \n\n\n\noverride fun onNewIntent(newIntent: Intent?) {\n  super.onNewIntent(intent)\n  intent = newIntent\n}  \n\n### 5. Approve order\nAfter your  CardRequest  has the card details, call  cardClient.approveOrder()  to process the payment.\n\n\n\nclass MyCardPaymentActivity: FragmentActivity {\n  fun cardCheckoutTapped(cardRequest: CardRequest) {\n    cardClient.approveOrder(this, cardRequest)\n  }\n}\n\n \n\n### 6. Handle payment result scenarios\nSet up your  ApproveOrderListener  to handle successful payments, errors, cancellations, and 3D Secure transaction flows.\n\n \n\n\n\nclass MyCardPaymentActivity: FragmentActivity, ApproveOrderListener {\n  fun cardCheckoutTapped(cardRequest: CardRequest) {\n    val result = cardClient.approveOrder(this, cardRequest)\n  }\n  fun setupCardClient() {\n    cardClient.listener = this\n  }\n  fun onApproveOrderSuccess(result: CardResult) {\n    // order was approved and is ready to be captured/authorized (see step 6)\n  }\n  fun onApproveOrderFailure(error: PayPalSDKError) {\n    // inspect 'error' for more information\n  }\n  fun onApproveOrderCanceled() {\n    // 3D Secure flow was canceled\n  }\n  fun onApproveOrderThreeDSecureWillLaunch() {\n    // 3D Secure flow will launch\n  }\n  fun onApproveOrderThreeDSecureDidFinish() {\n    // 3D Secure auth did finish successfully\n  }\n}\n\n### 7. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your  ORDER_ID  for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the  onApproveOrderSuccess  method.\n\nCall the  [authorize](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\n \n\n\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw ''\n\nCall the  [capture](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Capture order\n \n\n\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw ''\n\n \n\n### 8. Test integration\n\n\nBefore going live, test your integration in the  [sandbox environment](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/) .\n\nLearn more about the following resources on the  [Card Testing](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/)  page:\n\n- Use  [test card numbers](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/)  to simulate successful payments for Expanded Checkout integrations.\n- Use  [rejection triggers](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-rejectiontriggers)  to simulate card error scenarios.\n- Test  [3D Secure authentication](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-simulate3dsecurecardpayments)  scenarios.\n- Test your integration by following  [these recommended use cases](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-testintegration) . See the  [Orders v2 API](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/)  for details about billing address fields and other parameters. For example, use the  [2-character country code](https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/reference/country-codes/)  to test the billing address.\n\n**Note:**  Use the  [credit card generator](https://developer.paypal.com/tools/sandbox/card-testing/#link-creditcardgenerator)  to generate additional test credit cards for sandbox testing.\n\nWhen prompted for required data for the sandbox business request, such as a phone number, enter any number that fits the required format. Because this is a sandbox request, the data doesn't have to be factual.\n\nBefore you go live, you'll need to complete  [live onboarding](https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/entry/product/ppcp)  to be eligible to process cards with your live PayPal account.\n\n \n\n\n## Native Payments\n\n\n**Deprecation notice:**  The  PayPalNativePayments  module is deprecated since July 2024. Updates and bug fixes end in July 2025. We recommend to use the PayPalWebPayments module instead. To migrate from PayPalNativePayments to PayPalWebPayments , follow the steps in [Web payments](#web-payments) .\n\n### Use PayPal native payments\nUse  PayPalNativePayments  to add a PayPal paysheet to your app. The paysheet is a checkout page that the client launches within your app, instead of showing up as a pop-up. The paysheet shows all the PayPal payment methods available and helps the payer complete their payment.\n\n#### Native checkout for a first-time customer\n![img](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_01.png)  ![img](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-first-time-flow_02.png)\n\n#### Native checkout for a returning customer\n![img](https://www.paypalobjects.com/devdoc/iOS_SDK_native-checkout-repeat-time-flow.png)\n\nFollow these steps to add  PayPalNativePayments :\n\n \n\n### 1. Add PayPalNativePayments module to your app\nAdd the  paypal-native-payments  package dependency in your app's  build.gradle  file:\n\n \n\n\n\ndependencies {\n  implementation \"com.paypal.android:paypal-native-payments:CURRENT-VERSION\"\n}  Add the following Cardinal SDK Maven repository to your projects top-level build.gradle file to pass credentials to Gradle: \n\nallprojects {\n  repositories {\n    maven {\n      url  \"https://cardinalcommerceprod.jfrog.io/artifactory/android\"\n      credentials {\n        username \"<YOUR_JFROG_USERNAME>\"\n        password \"<YOUR_JFROG_PASSWORD>\"\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n \n\n### 2. Enable Native Checkout SDK\nYou'll need to set up authorization to use the Native Checkout SDK. To create a client ID and secret, follow the steps in  [Get Started](https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/#link-getstarted) . You need these values to generate an  ACCESS_TOKEN .\n\n#### Sandbox business account\nSet up your sandbox business account to use native checkout as follows:\n\n- Log into the  [**PayPal Developer Dashboard**](https://developer.paypal.com/dashboard/) , toggle  **Sandbox** , and go to  **Apps \u0026 Credentials** .\n- In  **REST API apps** , select the name of your app.\n- Go to  **Features**  \u0026gt;  **Accept payments**  and select  ***Native Checkout SDK** .\n- Select  **Save Changes** .\n\n#### Add return URL\nA return URL redirects users to the app after authenticating. Use the following steps to create a return URL:\n\n- Select your app from the  **My Apps \u0026 Credentials**  page on the Developer Dashboard.\n- Go to  **Features**  \u0026gt;  **Other features** . Select the  **Log in with PayPal**  checkbox. Click on  **Advanced Settings** . A pop-up window will open, and you'll see the  **Return URL**  field in the new window.\n\n- You can use an  [Android App Link](https://developer.android.com/training/app-links)  registered within the Developer Console to handle SDK redirects.\n\n- Alternatively, you can use your application ID (typically referenced via  BuildConfig.APPLICATION_ID ) and register your return URL with  ://paypalpay  as the suffix. For example, if your application ID is  com.paypal.app , input  com.paypal.app://paypalpay  as the return URL.\n- The return URL in the Developer Dashboard and the SDK must match exactly.\n- The application ID and return URL must use lower case letters. The return URL is passed to the SDK via an intent filter and  [host name matching in the Android framework is case-sensitive](https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/data-element#:~:text=Host%20name%20matching%20in%20the%20Android%20framework%20is%20case%2Dsensitive%2C%20unlike%20the%20formal%20RFC.%20As%20a%20result%2C%20always%20specify%20host%20names%20using%20lowercase%20letters)\n\n**Note:**  If you change the return URL in the Developer Dashboard, PayPal must review your app again. The review period automatically begins any time the return URL changes.\n\n- Select the  **Full Name**  and  **Email**  checkboxes found within the  **Advanced Settings** . These are scopes of the  [Identity API](https://developer.paypal.com/api/identity/v1/) .\n\n \n\n### 3. Create PayPalNativeCheckoutClient\nUse the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:\n\n \n\n#### 1. Construct CoreConfig\nIn your Android app, use the  CLIENT_ID  to construct a  CoreConfig .\n\n \n\n\n\nval coreConfig = CoreConfig(\"CLIENT_ID\", environment = Environment.SANDBOX)\n\n \n\n#### 2. Create native checkout request\nCreate a  PayPalNativeCheckoutClient  request to approve an order with a PayPal payment method and include the  RETURN_URL :\n\n \n\n\n\nval payPalNativeClient = PayPalNativeCheckoutClient(\n  application = requireActvitiy().application,\n  coreConfig = coreConfig,\n  returnUrl = \"RETURN_URL\"\n)\n\n \n\n#### 3. Set up payment listener\nImplement the  PayPalNativeCheckoutListener  on the  PayPalNativeCheckoutClient  to listen for result notifications from the SDK.\n\n \n\n\n\npayPalNativeClient.listener = object : PayPalNativeCheckoutListener {\n  override fun onPayPalCheckoutStart() {\n    // the PayPal paysheet is about to show up\n  }\n  override fun onPayPalCheckoutSuccess(result: PayPalNativeCheckoutResult) {\n    // order was approved and is ready to be captured/authorized\n  }\n  override fun onPayPalCheckoutFailure(error: PayPalSDKError) {\n    // handle the error\n  }\n  override fun onPayPalCheckoutCanceled() {\n    // the user canceled the flow\n  }\n}\n\n \n\n#### 4. Listen for shipping details\nWhen a payer chooses to use shipping details from their PayPal profile, use  PayPalNativeShippingListener  to listen for changes to their shipping address or shipping method.\n\nYou can only implement  PayPalNativeShippingListener  if the  [shipping_preference](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#definition-experience_context_base)  in the order ID is set to  GET_FROM_FILE.\n\n**Note:**  Skip this step if you created your order ID with the  shipping_preference  set to  NO_SHIPPING  or  SET_PROVIDED_ADDRESS .\n\nSet a  shippingListener  on the  PayPalNativeCheckoutClient  to send notifications to your app when the user updates their shipping address or shipping method.\n\nThis code sample uses a  trycatch  function to handle the response:\n\n \n\n\n\npayPalNativeClient.shippingListener = object : PayPalNativeShippingListener {\n  override fun onPayPalNativeShippingAddressChange(\n    actions: PayPalNativePaysheetActions,\n    shippingAddress: PayPalNativeShippingAddress\n  ) {\n    // called when the user updates their chosen shipping address\n    // you must call actions.approve() or actions.reject() in this callback\n    actions.approve()\n    // OPTIONAL: you can optionally patch your order. Once complete, call actions.approve() if successful or actions.reject() if not.\n  }\n  override fun onPayPalNativeShippingMethodChange(\n    actions: PayPalNativePaysheetActions,\n    shippingMethod: PayPalNativeShippingMethod\n  ) {\n    // called when the user updates their chosen shipping method\n    // patch your order server-side with the updated shipping amount.\n    // Once complete, call `actions.approve()` or `actions.reject()`\n    try {\n      // TODO: patch order on server side, notify SDK of success by calling actions.approve()\n      actions.approve()\n    } catch (e: Exception) {\n      // catch any errors from patching the order e.g. network unavailable\n      // and notify SDK that the update was unsuccessful\n      actions.reject()\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n \n\n#### 5. Modify shipping details\n\n\nWhen the shipping method changes, update the order details on your server by sending a  PATCH  request to the  [Update order](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch)  endpoint of the Orders API.\n\nApprove or reject changes to the shipping information to see changes appear in the paysheet UI by calling either  PayPalNativePaysheetActions.approve()  or  PayPalNativePaysheetActions.reject() .\n\nTo update the paysheet with a new shipping method, or when  onPayPalNativeShippingMethodChange  is called:\n\n- Patch the order on your server using the  replace  operation with all shipping methods. - Mark the new shipping method as selected.\n- Optional: Update the amount to reflect the new shipping cost.\n\n \n- Call  approve()  or  reject()  to accept or reject the changes and continue the payment flow.\n\nFor more information, visit the  [Update order](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_patch)  endpoint of the Orders v2 API.\n\n### 4. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an  ORDER_ID  by using the  [Orders v2 API](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your  ACCESS_TOKEN  in the  Authorization  header. To get an  ACCESS_TOKEN , use the  [Authentication API](https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/authentication/) . **Note:**  This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to  [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n \n- Pass the  intent . You'll need to pass either  AUTHORIZE  or  CAPTURE  as the  intent  type. This type must match the  /authorize  or  /capture  endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n \n\n\n#### **`Sample request`**\n```javascript\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw '{\n    \"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",\n    \"purchase_units\": [\n      {\n        \"amount\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"5.00\"\n        }\n      }\n    ]\n  }'\n\n```\n\n\n#### **`Sample response`**\n```javascript\n\n{\n  \"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",\n  \"status\":\"CREATED\"\n}\n\n```\nWhen a buyer starts a payment, send the  ORDER_ID  from your server to your client app.\n\n \n\n### 5. Start PayPal Native Payments flow\nTo start the PayPal Native Payments flow, call the  startCheckout  function in  PayPalNativeCheckoutClient , with a  PayPalNativeCheckoutRequest :\n\nval request = PayPalNativeCheckoutRequest(\"ORDER_ID\")\npaypalNativeClient.startCheckout(request)\n\n \n\n### 6. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your  ORDER_ID  for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the  onPayPalSuccess  method.\n\nCall the  [authorize](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\n \n\n\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw ''\n\nCall the  [capture](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Capture order\n \n\n\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw ''\n## Web payments\n### PayPal Web Payments\nIntegrate  PayPalWebPayments  to add a lighter checkout integration to your app. The checkout experience is launched in a browser within your application, reducing the size of the SDK.\n\nFollow these steps to integrate  PayPalWebPayments :\n\n \n\n### 1. Add PayPalWebPayments to your app\nAdd the  paypal-web-payments  package dependency in your app's  build.gradle  file:\n\ndependencies {\n      implementation \"com.paypal.android:paypal-web-payments:CURRENT-VERSION\"\n    } \n\n### 2. Set up your app for browser switching\nPayPalWebPayments  launches a checkout page in a browser within your application. Your app needs to handle the browser switch between the checkout page and your app. Set up a return URL that returns to your app from the browser.\n\nUpdate your app's  AndroidManifest.xml  with details about the card payment activity that will return the user to your app after completing the payment. Include the following elements:\n\n- Set the activity  launchMode  to  singleTop .\n- Set the  android:scheme  on the Activity that will be responsible for handling the deep link back into the app.\n- Add an  intent-filter .\n- Register the  myapp://  custom URL scheme in the  intent-filter .\n\nNote:  android:exported  is required if your app compile SDK version is API 31 (Android 12) or later.\n\n\u0026lt;activity android:name=\"com.company.app.MyPaymentsActivity\" android:exported=\"true\" android:launchmode=\"singleTop\"\u0026gt;\n              ...\n      \u0026lt;intent-filter\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;action android:name=\"android.intent.action.VIEW\"\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;data android:scheme=\"custom-url-scheme\"\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;category android:name=\"android.intent.category.DEFAULT\"\u0026gt;\n        \u0026lt;category android:name=\"android.intent.category.BROWSABLE\"\u0026gt;\n      \u0026lt;/category\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/category\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/data\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/action\u0026gt;\u0026lt;/intent-filter\u0026gt;\n \u0026lt;/activity\u0026gt;Also, add  onNewIntent  to the host activity in your app:\n\noverride fun onNewIntent(newIntent: Intent?) {\n      super.onNewIntent(intent)\n      intent = newIntent\n    } \n\n### 3. Create PayPalWebCheckoutClient\nUse the following steps to set up the PayPal Native Checkout client for your app:\n\n#### 1. Construct CoreConfig\nIn your Android app, use the  CLIENT_ID  to construct a  CoreConfig .\n\nval config = CoreConfig(\"CLIENT_ID\", environment = Environment.SANDBOX) \n\n#### 2. Create return URL\nSet a return URL using the custom scheme you configured in the  ActivityManifest.xml :\n\nval returnUrl = \"custom-url-scheme\" \n\n#### 3. Create web checkout request\nCreate a  PayPalWebCheckoutClient  to approve an order with a PayPal payment method:\n\nval payPalWebCheckoutClient = PayPalWebCheckoutClient(requireActivity(), config, returnUrl) \n\n#### 4. Set up payment listener\nSet a  PayPalWebCheckoutListener  on the client to receive payment flow callbacks:\n\npayPalWebCheckoutClient.listener = object : PayPalWebCheckoutListener {\n      override fun onPayPalWebSuccess(result: PayPalWebCheckoutResult) {\n        // order was approved and is ready to be captured/authorized (see step 7)\n      }\n      override fun onPayPalWebFailure(error: PayPalSDKError) {\n        // handle the error\n      }\n      override fun onPayPalWebCanceled() {\n        // the user canceled the flow\n      }\n    }**Note:**  Collecting a billing address can reduce the number of authentication challenges to customers.\n\n \n\n### 4. Get Order ID\nOn your server:\n\n- Create an  ORDER_ID  by using the  [Orders v2 API](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2) .\n- Pass your  ACCESS_TOKEN  in the  Authorization  header. To get an  ACCESS_TOKEN , use the  [Authentication API](https://developer.paypal.com/api/rest/authentication/) . **Note:**  This access token is only for the sandbox environment. When you're ready to go live, request a live access token by changing the request sandbox endpoint to  [https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token](https://api-m.paypal.com/v1/oauth2/token) .\n\n \n- Pass the  intent . You'll need to pass either  AUTHORIZE  or  CAPTURE  as the  intent  type. This type must match the  /authorize  or  /capture  endpoint you use to process your order.\n\n\n#### **`Sample request`**\n```javascript\n\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/' \\\n  -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n  -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n  --data-raw '{\n    \"intent\": \"CAPTURE|AUTHORIZE\",\n    \"purchase_units\": [\n      {\n        \"amount\": {\n          \"currency_code\": \"USD\",\n          \"value\": \"5.00\"\n        }\n      }\n    ]\n  }'\n\n```\n\n\n#### **`Sample response`**\n```javascript\n\n{\n \"id\":\"ORDER_ID\",\n \"status\":\"CREATED\"\n}\n\n```\nWhen a buyer starts a payment, send the  ORDER_ID  from your server to your client app.\n\n \n\n### 5. Create web checkout request\nConfigure your  PayPalWebCheckoutRequest  with the  ORDER_ID . You can also specify one of the following funding sources for your order:  PayPal  (default),  PayLater , or  PayPalCredit .\n\nval payPalWebCheckoutRequest = PayPalWebCheckoutRequest(\"ORDER_ID\", fundingSource = PayPalWebCheckoutFundingSource.PAYPAL) \n\n### 6. Approve order\nCall  payPalWebCheckoutClient.start()  to process the payment.\n\nclass MyCardPaymentActivity: FragmentActivity {\n      fun payPalWebCheckoutTapped(payPalWebCheckoutRequest: PayPalWebCheckoutRequest) {\n        payPalWebCheckoutClient.start(payPalWebCheckoutRequest)\n      }\n    } \n\n### 7. Authorize and capture order\nSubmit your  ORDER_ID  for authorization or capture when the PayPal Android SDK calls the  onPayPalWebSuccess  method on  PayPalWebCheckoutListener .\n\nCall the  [authorize](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_authorize)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to place the money on hold:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Authorize order\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/authorize' \\\n      -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n      -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n      --data-raw '' \n\nCall the  [capture](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/api/orders/v2/#orders_capture)  endpoint of the Orders V2 API to capture the money immediately:\n\n \n\n#### Sample request: Capture order\ncurl --location --request POST 'https://api-m.sandbox.paypal.com/v2/checkout/orders/ORDER_ID/capture' \\\n      -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \\\n      -H 'Authorization: Bearer ACCESS_TOKEN' \\\n      --data-raw ''\n\n## Payment buttons and fraud protection \nAfter you integrate a payment method, add a payment button to your page to start the payment process. You can also add fraud protection to your app.\n\n\n### Payment buttons\n### Use PayPal buttons in your UI\nThe  PaymentButtons  module provides a set of PayPal-branded buttons to seamlessly integrate with PayPal  web  and  native  payments.\n\nFollow these steps to add PayPal buttons to your integration:\n\n### 1. Add PaymentButtons to your app\nAdd the  payment-buttons  package dependency in your app's  build.gradle  file:\n\n1dependencies{2implementation\"com.paypal.android:payment-buttons:CURRENT-VERSION\"3}### 2. Create PayPal button\nThe  PaymentButtons  module provides 3 buttons that you can use in your application:\n\n- PayPalButton : A generic PayPal button.\n- PayPalPayLater : A PayPal button with a PayLater label.\n- PayPalCredit : A PayPal button with the PayPalCredit logo.\n\nThese buttons include customization options such as color, edges, size, and labels. Here's how to style the button corner radius:\n\n| Value | Description | Button |\n| --- | --- | --- |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/android/#rectanglebutton-shape-with-sharp-corners.)rectangle | Button shape with sharp corners. |  |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/android/#roundedrecommendedbutton-shape-with-rounded-corner-radius.-the-default-button-shape.)rounded | **Recommended** Button shape with rounded corner radius. The default button shape. |  |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/android/#pillbutton-in-pill-shape.)pill | Button in pill shape. |  |\n| [](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/android/#customcornerradiuscustomize-the-button's-corner-radius.-the-minimum-value-is-10-px-and-is-applied-to-all-4-corners.)customCornerRadius | Customize the button's corner radius. The minimum value is 10 px and is applied to all 4 corners. |  |\n\nAdd  PayPalButton  to your layout XML:\n\n1\u0026lt;com.paypal.android.paymentbuttons.PayPalButton2android:id=\"@+id/paypal_button\"3android:layout_width=\"match_parent\"4android:layout_height=\"wrap_content\"/\u0026gt;### 3. Reference PayPal button\nAdd the PayPal button to your code:\n\n1valpayPalButton=findViewById\u0026lt;PayPalButton\u0026gt;(R.id.paypal_button)2payPalButton.setOnClickListener{3// start the PayPal web or native4}\n,### Fraud protection\n### Protect from fraud\nThe  FraudProtection  module helps you collect data about a customer's device and match it with a session identifier on your server. For more information, see  [Fraud protection](https://developer.paypal.com/docs/checkout/advanced/customize/fraud-protection/) .\n\n**Note:**  If you integrated 3D Secure before June 2020, the  liabilityShifted ,  authenticationStatus , and  AuthenticationReason  parameters are no longer supported, but continue to work on the server.\n\n### 1. Add FraudProtection to your app\nAdd the  fraud-protection  package dependency in your app's  build.gradle  file:\n\ndependencies {\n  implementation \"com.paypal.android:fraud-protection:CURRENT-VERSION\"\n}### 2. Create PayPalDataCollector\nIn your Android app:\n\n- Use the  CLIENT_ID  to construct a  CoreConfig .\n- Construct a  PayPalDataCollector  using your  CoreConfig  object.\n\nval config = CoreConfig(\"CLIENT_ID\", environment = Environment.SANDBOX)\nval dataCollector = PayPalDataCollector(coreConfig = coreConfig)### 3. Collect client metadata\nCollect the client metadata ID before starting a payment from a mobile device:\n\n**Important:**   **User Data Consent**   Merchant applications are responsible for collecting user data consent. If your app has obtained consent from the user to collect location data in compliance with  [Google Play Developer Program policies](https://support.google.com/googleplay/android-developer/answer/10144311#personal-sensitive) , set  hasUserLocationConsent  to  true . This flag enables PayPal to collect necessary information required for Fraud Detection and Risk Management.     **Merchant App Disclosure**   Merchant applications may be required to display a disclosure before collecting user location data in accordance with Googles  [Best practices for prominent disclosures and consent](https://support.google.com/googleplay/android-developer/answer/11150561?hl=en\u0026ref_topic=12797379\u0026sjid=10421482417907285178-NC) . By setting  hasUserLocationConsent  to  true , your app is enabled to share device location data with a third party (PayPal) for Fraud Detection and Risk Management.\n\nval dataCollectorRequest = PayPalDataCollectorRequest(hasUserLocationConsent)\nval clientMetadataId = payPalDataCollector.collectDeviceData(context, dataCollectorRequest)Pass the result to your server, and include the client metadata ID in the payment request you send to PayPal. Don't cache or store this value.\n\n\n\n\n## Go live \nIf you have fulfilled the requirements for accepting Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments for your [business account](https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/bundle/business/upgrade) , review the [Move your app to production](/api/rest/production/) page to learn how to test and go live.\n    If this is your first time testing in a live environment, follow these steps:\n\n- Log into the [PayPal Developer Dashboard](/dashboard/) with your PayPal business account.\n- Complete [production onboarding](https://www.paypal.com/bizsignup/entry?_ga=1.171321763.248280996.1670866755) so you can process card payments with your live PayPal business account.\n- Request [Advanced Credit and Debit Card Payments](https://www.paypal.com/signin/client?flow=provisionUser\u0026country.x=US\u0026locale.x=en_US\u0026_ga=1.95899167.248280996.1670866755) for your business account.\n\n\n**info**\n**Important:** The code for the integration checks eligibility requirements, so the payment card fields only display when the production request is successful.\n\n"},"routes/__docs-pages":null},"actionData":null,"errors":null},"future":{"v2_dev":true,"unstable_postcss":false,"unstable_tailwind":false,"v2_errorBoundary":false,"v2_headers":false,"v2_meta":true,"v2_normalizeFormMethod":true,"v2_routeConvention":false}};</script><script nonce="OLqMZtrqsxMMCrbGwO7+cVjPT/fR/0siPvl5m1Ek0hWw+EsQ" type="module" async="">import "https://www.paypalobjects.com/ppdevdocs/bundles/10.6.8/manifest-2AA28ED2.js";

xhr.onreadystatechange = function () { if (xhr.readyState > 3 && xhr.status === 200) { try { if (xhr?.response && xhr.response != "OK") { const invalidCookies = JSON.parse(xhr?.response)?.invalidCookies; if (invalidCookies.length > 0) { const hostName = document.location.hostname; let subDomains = [hostName]; const parts = hostName.split('.'); parts.forEach((e, i) => {  if(e !== "www"){ subDomains.push("." + parts.slice(i).join('.')); } }); subDomains.pop(); invalidCookies.forEach(cookie => { document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=.paypal.com'; document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT;'; subDomains.forEach(domain => { document.cookie = cookie + '=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:01 GMT; domain=' + domain; }) }) } } } catch (error) { } } }; xhr.setRequestHeader('Accept', 'application/json'); xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json'); xhr.send(); }; function cookieFiltering(eventSource="cookieBanner"){ if(!true || false){ return; } cookieFilteringRequest(eventSource); } function postAjax(isFptiDataAvailable , cookieObj ) { if(!isFptiDataAvailable && getFptiReqData()){  isFptiDataAvailable = true; } if(isFptiDataAvailable){ acceptDeclineFptiEvents(cookieObj); } var xhr = window.XMLHttpRequest ? new XMLHttpRequest() : new ActiveXObject("Microsoft.XMLHTTP"); var endPoint = cookieObj.endPointPrefix + cookieObj.endPointSuffix; xhr.open('GET',endPoint); xhr.withCredentials = true; xhr.onreadystatechange = function() { if (xhr.readyState > 3 && xhr.status == 200) { cookieFiltering(cookieObj.eventSource); } }; xhr.setRequestHeader('Accept', 'application/json','Content-Type', 'application/json'); xhr.send(null); return xhr; }; function fptiRecordClick(bannerData){ window.PAYPAL.analytics.Analytics.prototype.recordClick({ data: {...bannerData, product:"cookieBanner"}}); }; function acceptDeclineFptiEvents(cookieObj){ var trackingPageName = '' || getFptiPage() || document.title; var cookiesText = cookieObj.cookiesText; var cookiePrefs = cookieObj.cookiePrefs; var eventName = cookieObj.eventName; var acEventName = cookieObj.acEventName; var bannerData = { e: 'cl', link: cookiesText, pglk: trackingPageName + '|' + cookiesText, pgln: trackingPageName + '|' + cookiesText, c_prefs: cookiePrefs, opsel: cookiePrefs + ',US', csource: 'cookie', event_name: eventName }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ bannerData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; fptiRecordClick(bannerData); var winFptiData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((window && window.fpti) || {})); var updatedFptiData = { cookiebannerhidden: 'true', c_prefs: cookiePrefs, event_name: acEventName }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ updatedFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; for(var key in updatedFptiData){ winFptiData[key] = updatedFptiData[key]; }; fptiLogActivity(winFptiData); }; function cookieObjSetup (type) { const cookieObjValue = { "accept" : { endPointSuffix : '&type=explicit_banner&country=US&policy=ccpa&version=v14', endPointPrefix : 'https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/privacy/cookiePrefs/accept?marketing=true&performance=true&functional=true', eventSource : 'acceptCookieBanner', cookiesText : 'acceptcookies', cookiePrefs : 'T=1,P=1,F=1,type=explicit_banner', eventName : 'cookie_banner_accept_clicked', acEventName : 'cookie_banner_accepted' }, "decline" : { endPointSuffix : '&type=explicit_banner&country=US&policy=ccpa&version=v14', endPointPrefix : 'https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/privacy/cookiePrefs/accept?marketing=false&performance=false&functional=false', eventSource : 'declineCookieBanner', cookiesText : 'declinecookies', cookiePrefs : 'T=0,P=0,F=0,type=explicit_banner', eventName : 'cookie_banner_decline_clicked', acEventName : 'cookie_banner_declined' }, "close" : { endPointSuffix : '&type=explicit_close&country=US&policy=ccpa&version=v14', endPointPrefix : 'https://www.paypal.com/myaccount/privacy/cookiePrefs/accept?marketing=true&performance=true&functional=true', eventSource : 'closeCookieBanner', cookiesText : 'closecookies', cookiePrefs : 'T=1,P=1,F=1,type=explicit_close', eventName : 'cookie_banner_close_clicked', acEventName : 'cookie_banner_closed' } }; return cookieObjValue[type]; } function bindGdprEvents () { var acceptAllButton = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var bannerDeclineButton = document.getElementById('bannerDeclineButton'); var bannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('bannerCloseButton'); var usBannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('usBannerCloseButton'); var manageCookiesLink = document.getElementById('manageCookiesLink'); var cookieStatement = document.getElementById('cookieStatement'); var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); var trackingPageName = '' || getFptiPage() || document.title; if (manageCookiesLink) { manageCookiesLink.onclick = function() { var manageCookiesData = { e: 'cl', link: 'managecookies', pglk: trackingPageName + '|managecookies', pgln: trackingPageName + '|managecookies', event_name: 'cookie_banner_manage_cookies_clicked' }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ manageCookiesData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; fptiRecordClick(manageCookiesData); }; } if (cookieStatement) { cookieStatement.onclick = function() { var cookieStatementData = { e: 'cl', link: 'cookieStmtLink', pglk: trackingPageName + '|cookieStmtLink', pgln: trackingPageName + '|cookieStmtLink', event_name: 'cookie_banner_cookie_statement_clicked' }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ cookieStatementData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; fptiRecordClick(cookieStatementData); }; } if(bannerCloseButton && cookieBanner && cookieLanguage){ bannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); setSessionStorage('isBannerClosed'); var closebannerFptiData = { e: 'cl', link: 'closeBanner', pglk: trackingPageName + '|closeBanner', pgln: trackingPageName + '|closeBanner', event_name: 'cookie_banner_close_clicked' }; for(var key in bannerFptiData){ closebannerFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; fptiRecordClick(closebannerFptiData); }; } if (acceptAllButton && cookieBanner && cookieLanguage) { acceptAllButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(true , cookieObjSetup('accept')); }; } if (bannerDeclineButton && cookieBanner && cookieLanguage) { bannerDeclineButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(true , cookieObjSetup('decline')); }; } if (usBannerCloseButton && cookieBanner && cookieLanguage) { usBannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(true , cookieObjSetup('close')); }; } window.hideGdprBanner = function () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if (cookieBannerUi && cookieBannerUi.className.indexOf('ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile') === -1) { cookieBannerUi.className += " ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile"; } }; window.showGdprBanner = function () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if (cookieBannerUi) { cookieBannerUi.className = cookieBannerUi.className.replace("ccpaHideCookieBannerMobile",""); } }; document.body.addEventListener("focus", function (event) { if (event.target.type === 'text' || event.target.type === 'number' || event.target.type === 'password' || event.target.type === 'email' || event.target.type === 'select-one') { window.hideGdprBanner(); } }, true); } function adjustPaddingTop(){ var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && bannerHeight){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingTop = bannerHeight/16 +'em'; } } }; var isPaddingBottomAdded = false, bannerPaddingBottom = ""; function adjustPaddingBottom(addListener){ if (undefined || !false) { return; } function adjustPaddingBottomEvent() { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll.length > 0){ var bodyPaddingBottom = cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom; var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0] && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none') { if (bodyPaddingBottom === "" || (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom === bodyPaddingBottom)) { var cookieBannerContainer = document.getElementsByClassName('ccpaCookieBanner_container'); var bannerBottomHeight = cookieBannerContainer.length > 0 ? parseInt(window.getComputedStyle(cookieBannerContainer[0]).bottom.replace("px", "")) : 0; var bannerHeight = cookieBanner ? cookieBanner.clientHeight : 0; bannerPaddingBottom = ((bannerHeight + bannerBottomHeight) / 16) + 'em'; cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom = bannerPaddingBottom; isPaddingBottomAdded = true; } else if (isPaddingBottomAdded && bannerPaddingBottom !== bodyPaddingBottom) { isPaddingBottomAdded = false; } } } } if (addListener) { adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent);  } else { var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingBottomEvent); adjustPaddingBottomEvent(); if (isPaddingBottomAdded && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.paddingBottom === bannerPaddingBottom) { cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-bottom'); } } } }; window.bindGdprEvents = bindGdprEvents; function cookieDisabled() { if (navigator.cookieEnabled === false) return "true"; else if (navigator.cookieEnabled === true) return "false"; else return "undefined"; }; function fptiLogActivity(winFptiData){ window.PAYPAL.analytics.Analytics.prototype.logActivity({...winFptiData, product:"cookieBanner"}); }; function gdprSetup () { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); var manageLink = document.getElementById('manageCookiesLink'); var acceptAllLink = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var trackingPageName = '' || getFptiPage() || document.title; if(!isBannerClosed()){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled";    } } var pageName = trackingPageName || getFptiPage() || document.title; var winFptiData = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify((window && window.fpti) || {})); if(false){ bannerFptiData.isNativeBannerHidden = true; } for(var key in bannerFptiData){ winFptiData[key] = bannerFptiData[key]; }; winFptiData['event_name'] = 'cookie_banner_shown'; fptiLogActivity(winFptiData); if (manageLink) { manageLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|managecookies')); } if (acceptAllLink) { acceptAllLink.setAttribute('pagename', (pageName + '|acceptcookies')); } bindGdprEvents(); }; function hideBanner() { var cookieLanguage = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieContent_wrapper'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if(cookieLanguage && cookieBanner){ cookieLanguage.style.display = 'none'; cookieBanner.style.display = 'none'; }else { return false; } window.removeEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop); var cookieBannerAcceptAll = document.getElementsByClassName("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"); if(cookieBannerAcceptAll && cookieBannerAcceptAll[0]){ cookieBannerAcceptAll[0].style.removeProperty('padding-top'); } document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll",""); document.body.className = document.body.className.replace("top-cookie-banner-enabled",""); return true; } function isPageReady () { var cookieBannerUi = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); return !!(cookieBannerUi && getFptiReqData()); } function enableFocusEvent(addListener){ if(!false || undefined){ return; } var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); function focusIn(e) { if(cookieBanner && cookieBanner.style.display != 'none'){ var activeElement = document.activeElement; if(((activeElement.getBoundingClientRect().bottom) > (cookieBanner.getBoundingClientRect().top)) && !activeElement.parentElement.nodeName.includes("UL")){ activeElement.scrollIntoView({block: 'center'}); } }else{ document.removeEventListener("focusin", focusIn); } } if(addListener){ document.addEventListener("focusin",focusIn); } } function enableEvents(enable){ adjustPaddingBottom(enable); enableFocusEvent(enable); } var maxRetries = 34, bannerhidden=false; function triggerBanner() { if (isPageReady()) { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } gdprSetup(); } else { if (isBannerClosed() && !bannerhidden ) { bannerhidden=hideBanner(); } if (maxRetries-- > 0) { setTimeout(triggerBanner, 150); } else { cookieFiltering('pageLoad'); if(true){setTimeout(function(){ cookieFiltering('afterPageLoad')}, 3000);} if (isBannerClosed()) { hideBanner(); } if(!isBannerClosed() && document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner') && !document.body.className.includes("ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll")){ document.body.className = document.body.className += " ccpaCookieBanner-acceptedAll"; if(undefined){ adjustPaddingTop(); window.addEventListener('resize', adjustPaddingTop);   document.body.className = document.body.className += " top-cookie-banner-enabled"; } } var acceptAllButton = document.getElementById('acceptAllButton'); var bannerDeclineButton = document.getElementById('bannerDeclineButton'); var bannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('bannerCloseButton'); var usBannerCloseButton = document.getElementById('usBannerCloseButton'); var cookieBanner = document.getElementById('ccpaCookieBanner'); if ( acceptAllButton ) { acceptAllButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('accept')); }; } if ( bannerDeclineButton ) { bannerDeclineButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('decline')); }; } if ( usBannerCloseButton ) { usBannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); if (false) { setSessionStorage('isUserAccepted'); } postAjax(false,cookieObjSetup('close')); }; } if ( bannerCloseButton ) { bannerCloseButton.onclick = function() { hideBanner(); setSessionStorage('isBannerClosed'); } } if(false){ setSessionStorage('isInvisibleBanner'); } } } } triggerBanner(); })();</script></div></body></html>
